model1.list <- lapply(dfKR_list, function(x) {
  try({model.obj <- feverDay_fit(x)})
  
  if(!exists("model.obj")) {
    model.obj <- NA
  }
  
  return(model.obj)
  
})

    cat("\n", svy.name)

    cat("\n", svy.name, " is not yet properly coded")
  }
}
